确乎能其事者而已矣,que'hu'neng'qi'shi'zhe'er'yi'yi
群生不夭,qun'sheng'bu'yao
然不顾,ran'bu'gu
然不免于患,ran'bu'mian'yu'huan
然不趋,ran'bu'qu
然不然,ran'bu'ran
然察其始而本无生,ran'cha'qi'shi'er'ben'wu'sheng
然臣有三剑,ran'chen'you'san'jian
然大也,ran'da'ye
然弟之哉,ran'di'zhi'zai
然而不可者,ran'er'bu'ke'zhe
然而不中者,ran'er'bu'zhong'zhe
然而道尽,ran'er'dao'jin
然而黄帝不能致德,ran'er'huang'di'bu'neng'zhi'de
然而巨盗至,ran'er'ju'dao'zhi
然而攫之者必有天下,ran'er'jue'zhi'zhe'bi'you'tian'xia
然而来而已矣,ran'er'lai'er'yi'yi
然而其中津津乎犹有恶也,ran'er'qi'zhong'jin'jin'hu'you'you'e'ye
然而田成子一旦杀齐君而盗其国,ran'er'tian'cheng'zi'yi'dan'sha'qi'jun'er'dao'qi'guo
然而田原不遇岁,ran'er'tian'yuan'bu'yu'sui
然而往,ran'er'wang
然而笑曰,ran'er'xiao'yue
然而夜半有力者负之而走,ran'er'ye'ban'you'li'zhe'fu'zhi'er'zou
然而至此极者,ran'er'zhi'ci'ji'zhe
然而指我则胜我,ran'er'zhi'wo'ze'sheng'wo
然放杖而笑,ran'fang'zhang'er'xiao
然后,ran'hou
然后拔其国,ran'hou'ba'qi'guo
然后成,ran'hou'cheng
然后从之者也,ran'hou'cong'zhi'zhe'ye
然后附之以文,ran'hou'fu'zhi'yi'wen
然后加手焉,ran'hou'jia'shou'yan
然后列子自以为未始学而归,ran'hou'lie'zi'zi'yi'wei'wei'shi'xue'er'gui
然后民始惑乱,ran'hou'min'shi'huo'luan
然后能独行,ran'hou'neng'du'xing
然后去性而从于心,ran'hou'qu'xing'er'cong'yu'xin
然后入山林,ran'hou'ru'shan'lin
然后调理四时,ran'hou'tiao'li'si'shi
然后图南,ran'hou'tu'nan
然乎,ran'hu
然惊曰,ran'jing'yue
然空然,ran'kong'ran
然难言哉,ran'nan'yan'zai
然疲役而不知其所归,ran'pi'yi'er'bu'zhi'qi'suo'gui
然其病病者犹未病也,ran'qi'bing'bing'zhe'you'wei'bing'ye
然岂可以贪爵禄而使吾君有妄施之名乎,ran'qi'ke'yi'tan'jue'lu'er'shi'wu'jun'you'wang'shi'zhi'ming'hu
然其失性均也,ran'qi'shi'xing'jun'ye
然且不免于罔罗机辟之患,ran'qie'bu'mian'yu'wang'luo'ji'pi'zhi'huan
然且世世称之曰,ran'qie'shi'shi'cheng'zhi'yue
然且语而不舍,ran'qie'yu'er'bu'she
冉求失问而退,ran'qiu'shi'wen'er'tui
冉求未对,ran'qiu'wei'dui
冉求问于仲尼曰,ran'qiu'wen'yu'zhong'ni'yue
然如将不得已,ran'ru'jiang'bu'de'yi
然若果然也,ran'ruo'guo'ran'ye
然若亡而存,ran'ruo'wang'er'cun
然身食肉而终,ran'shen'shi'rou'er'zhong
然随而哭之,ran'sui'er'ku'zhi
然为世俗之礼,ran'wei'shi'su'zhi'li
然吾王所见剑士,ran'wu'wang'suo'jian'jian'shi
然奚求焉,ran'xi'qiu'yan
然响然,ran'xiang'ran
冉相氏得其环中以随成,ran'xiang'shi'de'qi'huan'zhong'yi'sui'cheng
然已解,ran'yi'jie
然用力甚多而见功寡,ran'yong'li'shen'duo'er'jian'gong'gua
然有形,ran'you'xing
然犹有不胜也,ran'you'you'bu'sheng'ye
然于然,ran'yu'ran
然在,ran'zai
然则卜之,ran'ze'bo'zhi
然则厕足而垫之致黄泉,ran'ze'ce'zu'er'dian'zhi'zhi'huang'quan
然则朝四而暮三,ran'ze'chao'si'er'mu'san
然则吊焉若此可乎,ran'ze'diao'yan'ruo'ci'ke'hu
然则夫子何方之依,ran'ze'fu'zi'he'fang'zhi'yi
然则夫子何故未尝称之,ran'ze'fu'zi'he'gu'wei'chang'cheng'zhi
然则何贵于道邪,ran'ze'he'gui'yu'dao'xie
然则何如,ran'ze'he'ru
然则君之所读者,ran'ze'jun'zhi'suo'du'zhe
然则人固有尸居而龙见,ran'ze'ren'gu'you'shi'ju'er'long'jian
然则儒墨杨秉四,ran'ze'ru'mo'yang'bing'si
然则若何,ran'ze'ruo'he
然则是至乎,ran'ze'shi'zhi'hu
然则是至人之德已乎,ran'ze'shi'zhi'ren'zhi'de'yi'hu
然则孰可,ran'ze'shu'ke
然则俗故严于亲而尊于君邪,ran'ze'su'gu'yan'yu'qin'er'zun'yu'jun'xie
然则谓之道足乎,ran'ze'wei'zhi'dao'zu'hu
然则我何为乎,ran'ze'wo'he'wei'hu
然则我内直而外曲,ran'ze'wo'nei'zhi'er'wai'qu
然则我与若与人俱不能相知也,ran'ze'wo'yu'ruo'yu'ren'ju'bu'neng'xiang'zhi'ye
然则吾大天地而小豪末,ran'ze'wu'da'tian'di'er'xiao'hao'mo
然则吾奈何,ran'ze'wu'nai'he
然则物无知邪,ran'ze'wu'wu'zhi'xie
然则无用之为用也亦明矣,ran'ze'wu'yong'zhi'wei'yong'ye'yi'ming'yi
然则乡之所谓知者,ran'ze'xiang'zhi'suo'wei'zhi'zhe
然则有鬼乎,ran'ze'you'gui'hu
然则子无师邪,ran'ze'zi'wu'shi'xie
然执干而舞,ran'zhi'gan'er'wu
然卒为天下笑,ran'zu'wei'tian'xia'xiao
攘臂乎桎梏之间,rang'bi'hu'zhi'gu'zhi'jian
攘弃仁义,rang'qi'ren'yi
绕以渤海,rao'yi'bo'hai
扰则忧,rao'ze'you
人必反灾之,ren'bi'fan'zai'zhi
人不忘其所忘而忘其所不忘,ren'bu'wang'qi'suo'wang'er'wang'qi'suo'bu'wang
人不以善言为贤,ren'bu'yi'shan'yan'wei'xian
仁常而不成,ren'chang'er'bu'cheng
人臣之礼也,ren'chen'zhi'li'ye

人大喜邪,ren'da'xi'xie

任公子得若鱼,ren'gong'zi'de'ruo'yu
任公子为大钩巨缁,ren'gong'zi'wei'da'gou'ju'zi
人故无情乎,ren'gu'wu'qing'hu

人含其知,ren'han'qi'zhi
人乎,ren'hu
人惑则死,ren'huo'ze'si
人见而悦之者,ren'jian'er'yue'zhi'zhe
人见其,ren'jian'qi
人见其人,ren'jian'qi'ren
人皆为之,ren'jie'wei'zhi
人皆有七窍以视听食息此独无有,ren'jie'you'qi'qiao'yi'shi'ting'shi'xi'ci'du'wu'you

人哭亦哭,ren'ku'yi'ku
人籁则比竹是已,ren'lai'ze'bi'zhu'shi'yi
人类悲之,ren'lei'bei'zhi

人莫鉴于流水而鉴于止水,ren'mo'jian'yu'liu'shui'er'jian'yu'zhi'shui

人其尽死,ren'qi'jin'si
任其性命之情而已矣,ren'qi'xing'ming'zhi'qing'er'yi'yi
人且偃然寝于巨室,ren'qie'yan'ran'qin'yu'ju'shi

人生天地之间,ren'sheng'tian'di'zhi'jian
任士之所劳,ren'shi'zhi'suo'lao
人孰敢不听而化诸,ren'shu'gan'bu'ting'er'hua'zhu
人死者有时,ren'si'zhe'you'shi
人虽有知,ren'sui'you'zhi
人特以有君为愈乎己,ren'te'yi'you'jun'wei'yu'hu'ji
人谓之不死,ren'wei'zhi'bu'si
人谓之樗,ren'wei'zhi'chu
人谓之童子,ren'wei'zhi'tong'zi
衽席之上,ren'xi'zhi'shang
仁贤不肖袭情,ren'xian'bu'xiao'xi'qing
人相忘乎道术,ren'xiang'wang'hu'dao'shu
人相造乎道,ren'xiang'zao'hu'dao
人心排下而进上,ren'xin'pai'xia'er'jin'shang
仁也,ren'ye

仁义,ren'yi
人以其全足笑吾不全足者众矣,ren'yi'qi'quan'zu'xiao'wu'bu'quan'zu'zhe'zhong'yi
人亦无疵焉,ren'yi'wu'ci'yan

人有能游,ren'you'neng'you

人有心而兵有顺,ren'you'xin'er'bing'you'shun
人有修者,ren'you'xiu'zhe

人与之鉴,ren'yu'zhi'jian

人在外,ren'zai'wai

仁者居之,ren'zhe'ju'zhi

任知则民相盗,ren'zhi'ze'min'xiang'dao

人卒闻之,ren'zu'wen'zhi

日出多伪,ri'chu'duo'wei

日以心斗,ri'yi'xin'dou

日中穴,ri'zhong'xue
容成氏曰,rong'cheng'shi'yue

荣辱立然后睹所病,rong'ru'li'ran'hou'du'suo'bing
汝必躬服仁义而明言是非,ru'bi'gong'fu'ren'yi'er'ming'yan'shi'fei

若白驹之过隙,ruo'bai'ju'zhi'guo'xi

若伯夷,ruo'bo'yi

若此三年,ruo'ci'san'nian

若殆往而刑耳,ruo'dai'wang'er'xing'er
若殆为人灾夫,ruo'dai'wei'ren'zai'fu
若殆以不信厚言,ruo'dai'yi'bu'xin'hou'yan
若夫不刻意而高,ruo'fu'bu'ke'yi'er'gao
若父不能诏其子,ruo'fu'bu'neng'zhao'qi'zi
若夫藏天下于天下而不得所循,ruo'fu'cang'tian'xia'yu'tian'xia'er'bu'de'suo'xun

若负重行而上阪,ruo'fu'chong'xing'er'shang'ban

若夫万物之情,ruo'fu'wan'wu'zhi'qing
